### [347] [Low-Overhead Receiver Design for Data-Dependent Superimposed Training via Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29995)
*Xinjie Li,Xingyu Zhou,Jing Zhang,Chao-Kai Wen,Xiao Li,Shi Jin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于数据依赖叠加训练(DDST)的增强型传输框架，通过非迭代导频-数据解耦、混合传输方案及Vision Transformer神经接收机，在时变信道下以更低复杂度实现比现有SIP方案更优的性能增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 叠加导频(SIP)传输虽通过消除专用导频开销提升了频谱效率，但存在严重的导频-数据耦合问题，导致接收机面临性能与复杂度的瓶颈。

Method: 1) 针对准静态块衰落信道，利用数据依赖代数结构设计增强型DDST接收机实现非迭代解耦；2) 针对快时变环境，提出混合传输方案，在部分资源元上应用DDST，结合OP的无干扰传输与SIP的零导频开销优势；3) 设计基于Vision Transformer的神经接收机，捕获导频与含扰数据间的正交结构及信道相关性。

Result: 在低至中等信噪比区间、时变信道条件下，所提框架相比现有SIP接收机取得显著性能增益，同时具备更优的计算效率。

Conclusion: 所提出的DDST增强框架有效缓解了SIP的导频-数据耦合瓶颈，在复杂度和性能之间取得了更好的平衡，尤其适用于时变信道场景。

Abstract: Superimposed pilot (SIP) transmission improves spectral efficiency by eliminating the dedicated pilot overhead required in orthogonal pilot (OP)-based schemes. However, SIP suffers from severe pilot-data coupling, which leads to a critical performance-complexity bottleneck at the receiver. To address this issue, this paper proposes a low-overhead transmission framework that revitalizes data-dependent superimposed training (DDST) with enhanced interference mitigation strategies. First, for quasi-static block-fading channels, an enhanced DDST receiver is developed to achieve non-iterative pilot-data decoupling by exploiting data-dependent algebraic structures. Second, to overcome the sensitivity of conventional DDST to channel variations and symbol misidentification in fast time-varying environments, a mix transmission scheme is developed. By strategically applying DDST to a subset of resource elements, the proposed scheme combines the interference-free transmission property of OP with the zero-pilot-overhead advantage of SIP, thereby improving demapping reliability and interference suppression. Furthermore, under the proposed mix scheme, a Vision Transformer-based neural receiver is designed to capture the orthogonal structure between pilots and perturbation-bearing data, as well as the underlying channel correlations, thereby relaxing the stringent quasi-static assumption required for interference disentanglement. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves significant performance gains in the low-to-medium SNR regime under time-varying channels while providing superior computational efficiency compared with state-of-the-art SIP receivers.

</details>


### [348] [List Recovery for Random Low-Rate Linear Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30101)
*Isaac M Hair,Amit Sahai*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文证明了在足够大的素数域上，随机低速率线性码具有近乎最优的列表恢复保证：对于固定维度d、错误率α和精度参数ε，高概率下随机d维线性码能同时对所有输入列表大小ℓ ≤ 2^{O(n/log n)}实现(α, ℓ, (1+ε)/(1-α)·ℓ)-列表恢复。同时给出了下界，表明任何至少二维的线性码无法对ℓ ≥ 2^{Ω(n)}实现同样的列表恢复，证明了结果近乎最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机低速率线性码的列表恢复能力，并探索其理论极限。

Method: 受Matoušek等人关于从投影重构点集的工作启发，结合确定性图论证书、非零行列式判定准则以及Schwartz-Zippel引理进行证明。

Result: 随机d维线性码以高概率对所有ℓ ≤ 2^{O(n/log n)}实现(α, ℓ, (1+ε)/(1-α)·ℓ)-列表恢复；同时证明任何至少二维的线性码无法对ℓ ≥ 2^{Ω(n)}实现该性质的紧下界。

Conclusion: 该结果给出了随机低速率线性码列表恢复能力的近乎最优刻画。

Abstract: We prove a list recovery guarantee for random low-rate linear codes over sufficiently large prime fields. For fixed dimension $d$, error fraction $α$, and accuracy parameter $\varepsilon$, a random $d$-dimensional linear code $C \subseteq \mathbb{F}_p^n$ is, with high probability, $(α,\ell,\frac{1+\varepsilon}{1-α}\ell)$-list recoverable simultaneously for all input list sizes $\ell\le 2^{O_{α, \varepsilon, d}(n/\log n)}$. The proof is inspired by work of Matoušek, Přívětivý, and Škovroň on reconstructing point sets from their projections. It combines a deterministic graph-theoretic certificate, a nonvanishing determinant criterion, and the Schwartz--Zippel lemma. We also give a lower bound showing that any linear code $C \subseteq \mathbb{F}_p^n$ of dimension at least two cannot be $(α,\ell,\frac{1+\varepsilon}{1-α}\ell)$-list recoverable for feasible list sizes $\ell \geq 2^{Ω_{α, \varepsilon}(n)}$. In this sense, our result is nearly optimal.

</details>


### [349] [Majorization precursors to supermodularity and subadditivity on the majorization lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30331)
*Alexander Stévins,Michael G. Jabbour,Serge Deside,Nicolas J. Cerf*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文建立了在偏序格上的两种结构性质——超模性和次可加性——的“前驱”关系（precursors），证明所有凹函数之和（sum-concave函数）在majorization格上具有超模性和次可加性，并以此导出Tsallis熵（所有α）和Rényi熵（α>1）满足这些性质，同时恢复了Shannon熵的对应性质。进一步强化了这些不等式：所有熵泛函在majorization格上严格次可加；Tsallis熵（从而Shannon熵）在majorization格上严格超模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在majorization诱导的偏序格上建立超模性和次可加性的统一结构框架，揭示这些性质背后更基本的序关系（precursors），从而统一解释和推广各类熵泛函的单调性与不等式性质。

Method: 首先定义两种结构性的majorization关系（precursors），证明它们蕴含超模性和次可加性；然后证明所有sum-concave函数在上述格上满足这两种性质；最后将Tsallis熵、Rényi熵和Shannon熵表示为sum-concave函数，利用该框架导出相关不等式，并进一步证明严格版本。

Result: (1) Tsallis熵（所有α）和Rényi熵（α>1）在majorization格上超模且次可加；(2) 所有上述熵泛函严格次可加；(3) Tsallis熵（从而Shannon熵）严格超模。

Conclusion: 发现了一类更基础的序结构关系（precursors），为理解majorization格上熵泛函的超模性和次可加性提供了统一的理论框架，并证明了这些不等式在某些条件下的严格版本。

Abstract: We establish two structural majorization relations, which we call precursors, underlying the properties of supermodularity and subadditivity on the lattice induced by majorization. These are precursors in that they immediately imply that all sums of concave functions, which we dub sum-concave functions, are supermodular and subadditive on the majorization lattice. Using these majorization relations, we then show the supermodularity and subadditivity (in the lattice-theoretic sense) of Tsallis entropies (for all $α$) and Rényi entropies (for all $α> 1$), also recovering these properties for the Shannon entropy in the process. We further strengthen these inequalities, showing that: (i) all these entropic functionals are strictly subadditive on the majorization lattice; (ii) Tsallis entropies (and therefore the Shannon entropy as well) are strictly supermodular on the majorization lattice.

</details>

### [350] [Comparative Analysis of Compliance-Matrix Induced Norms in Structural Topology Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28857)
*Jyotiranjan Nayak,Shafeequdheen P,Vijayakrishna Rowthu*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文研究了结构拓扑优化中三种不同的柔度公式（经典二次柔度、l2范数平方根形式、l1范数形式）对优化结果的影响，发现经典公式产生分布良好的载荷路径，而l1公式则促进稀疏且高度局部化的结构构件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究基于不同范数表示的替代柔度公式对结构拓扑优化结果的影响，揭示目标函数选择对于优化景观和最终拓扑的关键作用。

Method: 分别采用三种柔度公式：经典二次柔度、对应l2范数的平方根形式、以及基于刚度加权位移场的谱l1范数形式，进行结构拓扑优化对比分析。

Result: 经典柔度公式产生载荷路径分布良好的拓扑结构；l1范数公式则促进稀疏且高度局部化的结构构件。

Conclusion: 目标函数的选择在拓扑优化中起关键作用，不同柔度公式可为实现特定结构性能提供定制化的优化策略。

Abstract: Compliance minimization is a central objective in structural topology optimization, commonly interpreted as the total strain energy of a system. In this work, we examine the influence of alternative compliance formulations based on different norm representations of structural energy. Specifically, we consider three formulations: the classical quadratic compliance, its square-root form corresponding to an l2 norm, and a spectral l1 -norm based formulation derived from the stiffness weighted displacement field. Although these formulations arise from the same stiffness displacement relationship, they generate markedly different optimization landscapes and result in distinct structural topologies. Numerical results indicate that the classical formulation produces well-distributed load paths, whereas the l1 -based formulation promotes sparse and highly localized structural members. These findings underscore the critical role of objective function selection in topology optimization and offer insights into alternative formulations for achieving tailored structural performance.

### [351] [An End-to-End PyTorch Interface for Differentiable PDE Solvers: A RANS Model-Correction Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28858)
*Luca Saverio,Michele Alessandro Bucci,Gianmarco Farro,Cédric Content,Denis Sipp*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在完全可微分的机器学习框架中求解偏微分方程约束逆问题的端到端策略，通过将PDE重新表述为隐式层并集成到PyTorch自动微分图中，实现了对可训练参数φ的优化。方法在可压缩流的RANS方程上进行了验证，包括NASA壁挂式鼓包和VKI LS-59涡轮叶片两个应用案例，展示了框架在湍流建模及更广泛的物理信息PDE约束问题中的灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的PDE约束逆问题求解通常需要手动推导伴随方程或设计复杂的数值优化流程，缺乏通用性和易用性。本文旨在提供一个统一、用户友好的端到端可微分框架，能够适用于从数据同化到闭合建模的广泛问题，降低将数据驱动组件与物理约束结合的门槛。

Method: 方法将基线可微PDE求解器（预测状态w满足R(w)=0）与参数化的可微校正项f_φ(w)结合。通过将PDE重新表述为隐式层（implicit layer），将其嵌入任意目标函数中，并利用PyTorch的自动微分图进行端到端优化。所有操作均在完全可微分的Python工作流中实现。

Result: 在2D NASA壁挂式鼓包测试案例中，成功优化了生产项参数以匹配时间平均LES数据；在VKI LS-59涡轮叶片案例中，通过优化可训练空间场重构了Spalart-Allmaras涡粘度场。结果表明框架具有灵活性，可适用于湍流建模之外的更广泛物理信息PDE约束问题。

Conclusion: 该框架为PDE约束逆问题提供了一种统一、灵活且用户友好的解决方案，证明了在可微编程范式下将数据驱动组件与物理模型无缝结合的有效性，拓展了数据驱动组件在物理信息PDE约束问题中的应用前景。

Abstract: This work presents an end-to-end strategy for solving inverse problems constrained by Partial Differential Equations within a fully differentiable Machine Learning framework. The proposed formulation provides a unified and user-friendly methodology applicable to a wide range of problems, from data assimilation to closure modeling. Our approach combines a baseline differentiable PDE solver, which predicts the state w from the nonlinear system $R(w) = 0$, with a generic additive, parametrized, and differentiable correction $f_φ(w)$, with trainable parameters $φ$. We show how to optimize phi within a fully differentiable Python workflow by reformulating the PDE as an implicit layer, enabling its integration into arbitrary objective functions, while leveraging PyTorch's automatic differentiation graph. The method is demonstrated on the Reynolds-Averaged Navier-Stokes equations for compressible flows, where the closure term, or a portion of it, is modeled using trainable parameters or a Neural Network. The first application considers the 2D NASA Wall-Mounted Hump test case, where a production-term parameter is optimized against time-averaged LES data. A second application is carried out on the VKI LS-59 turbine blade, where the Spalart-Allmaras eddy viscosity field is reconstructed through the optimization of a trainable spatial field. A dataset is generated starting from the VKI LS-59 turbine blade geometry using the differentiable BROADCAST solver with the Spalart-Allmaras turbulence model. The results highlight the flexibility of the framework, showing its applicability beyond turbulence modeling to a broader class of physics-informed PDE-constrained problems with data-driven components.

### [352] [Automated design of soft-rigid hybrid robots for dynamic locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29389)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种自动化设计方法，联合优化自由形态软体形状、刚性桁架布局和多通道驱动。构建可微仿真器，将物质点法（MPM）与扩展位置动力学（XPBD）耦合，实现基于梯度的搜索优化。优化生成桁架骨架以传递驱动力至软体，并制造优化设计在步行任务上评估。

Conclusion: 所提出的软-刚混合自动设计方法能够生成兼具柔顺性与承载能力的机器人结构，刚性骨架对驱动力的有效传递是实现预期运动模式的关键。

Abstract: Rigid-bodied robots often lack compliance needed to adapt to unstructured environments, while fully soft robots, though highly adaptable, struggle with scalability and load capacity. In nature, musculoskeletal systems balance strength and flexibility by integrating hard and soft tissues. Inspired by this principle, we present an automated design method for soft-rigid hybrids that optimizes a freeform soft-body shape, a stiff truss layout, and multi-channel actuation. Our differentiable simulator couples the material point method (MPM) for deformable bodies with extended position-based dynamics (XPBD) for truss elements, enabling gradient-based search. The optimization generates truss skeletons that transmit actuation forces to the soft body. We fabricate the optimized design and evaluate it on a walking task. Experiments reproduce the walking mode predicted by the optimization, which does not emerge without the skeleton. Modal analysis further suggests that the skeleton enables deformation modes near the actuation frequency that promote effective stride generation.

### [353] [Beyond TVL: An Explainable Risk Scoring Framework for Tokenized Real-World Assets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29689)
*Rischan Mafrur,Khadijah*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一个可解释的风险评分框架，从流动性风险、集中度风险和市场规模风险三个维度评估代币化现实世界资产（RWA），发现高TVL资产可能因低流动性、高集中度而隐含高风险，而参与度更广的资产即使估值较低也表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估多依赖TVL等粗放指标，但高资产规模不等于低风险，代币化资产可能存在流动性不足、交易薄弱或高度集中的问题，需要更精细的风险量化方法。

Method: 基于RWA.xyz公开数据，构建一个三維可解释风险评分框架，涵盖流动性风险（L）、集中度风险（C）和市场质量风险（M），使用换手率、持有者分布、活跃地址数、转账频率及赫芬达尔指数等可观测指标。

Result: 多个高链上价值的RWA代币因转账活动有限、换手率低、所有权集中而表现出高风险；而参与更广、链上活动更强的资产即使TVL较小，流动性和集中度风险也更低。

Conclusion: TVL单一指标会掩盖代币化资产市场的重要风险，该数据驱动的透明评分方法可为资产比较和风险评估提供更可靠的实证基础。

Abstract: Tokenized real-world assets (RWAs) are often evaluated through headline indicators such as total value locked (TVL) or on-chain asset value. However, a large asset base does not necessarily imply low risk, since tokenized assets may remain illiquid, weakly traded, or highly concentrated among a small number of holders. Using public data from RWA.xyz, this paper develops an empirical and explainable risk scoring framework for tokenized RWA markets. The framework evaluates three dimensions of risk: liquidity risk $L$, concentration risk $C$, and market-quality risk $M$. These risk dimensions are constructed from observable indicators, including turnover, holder distribution, active-address activity, transfer frequency, and network concentration measured through Herfindahl indices. The analysis shows that several RWA tokens with substantial on-chain value exhibit high empirical risk because they combine limited transfer activity, low turnover, and concentrated ownership structures. In contrast, assets with broader participation and stronger on-chain activity display lower liquidity and concentration risk, even when their headline asset values are smaller. The findings demonstrate that TVL alone can obscure important risks in tokenized asset markets. By providing a transparent and data-driven risk scoring approach, this paper contributes to the empirical assessment of RWA liquidity and offers a practical basis for comparing tokenized assets beyond headline valuation metrics.

### [354] [A Lumped RC Equivalent Circuit Model of Head Tissues in sub-MHz Frequency Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29996)

Method: 提出一种集总RC等效电路模型，采用三层球头几何结构，引入复电导率在电准静态（EQS）框架下处理频率相关的组织电导率和介电常数，使用最小化阻抗元件集表示电信号传播机制，并通过偶极子脑源配置进行验证。

Result: 模型在不同颅骨厚度和偶极子偏心率下，头皮电压峰值估计与半解析解高度一致；定量评估表明组织色散和位移电流对模型精度有显著贡献。

Conclusion: 所提出的集总RC等效电路模型在高达50 kHz频率范围内能够准确再现三层球头几何结构的电学行为，为快速原型设计、实时仿真和电路级集成提供了计算高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Accurate modeling of electric potential and current distribution in head tissues is crucial for the design and evaluation of neuro-sensing and neuro-stimulation systems operating in the sub megahertz frequency range. Numerical methods are widely employed in electromagnetic simulations, however their computational cost can limit their applicability to rapid prototyping, real-time simulations, and circuit-level integration. In this work, we introduce a lumped RC equivalent circuit model that reproduces the electrical behavior of a canonical three-layer spherical head geometry over a frequency range up to 50 kHz. The model accounts for frequency-dependent tissue conductivity and permittivity to capture dispersive effects, employing complex conductivity in the electro-quasi-static (EQS) regime. The circuit topology uses a minimal set of impedance elements in order to represent the essential mechanisms of electric signal propagation. Validation was performed using a dipolar brain source configuration for scalp voltage peak estimation, showing close agreement with semi-analytical solutions across different skull thicknesses and dipole eccentricities. In addition, the impact of tissue dispersion and displacement current inclusion on the model accuracy was quantitatively assessed, highlighting their contribution to the overall fidelity of the proposed approach.

</details>

Motivation: 传统EQS头部模型计算复杂，需要一种计算高效的紧凑电路模型来近似多层头部组织的电特性，同时准确捕捉频率相关的色散效应。

Method: 采用三层球壳几何（脑、颅骨、头皮），每层用径向和切向RC分支电路建模，将频率依赖的组织电导率和介电常数映射为色散的阻容元件。

Result: 模型与半解析球谐参考解在不同几何配置和频率下吻合良好；忽略色散和电容路径会导致头皮电位被高估。

Conclusion: 色散RC电路建模对于准确估计头皮电位是必要的，所提出的紧凑电路可作为EQS头部建模的有效替代方案。

Abstract: In this work, we present a compact surrogate circuit for electro-quasi-static (EQS) head modeling. A three-shell geometry (brain, skull, scalp) is considered, and each layer is modeled through radial and tangential pathways, implemented as RC branches. Frequency-dependent tissue conductivity and permittivity are mapped into dispersive resistive and capacitive elements. The model is validated against a semi-analytical spherical-harmonics reference solution over multiple geometrical configurations and operating frequencies, demonstrating good agreement. Neglecting dispersion and capacitive pathways can lead to an overestimation of scalp potentials over the considered frequency range, highlighting the need for dispersive RC circuit modeling.

</details>
